catc0n at 2024-12-16T13:02:28.414Z ##

Full Rapid7 analysis of #Cleo CVE-2024-55956 now available c/o @stephenfewer. It's neither a patch bypass of CVE-2024-50623 nor part of a chain after all — totally new bug, different exploitation strategies across the two issues (though the same endpoint gets used either way).

I'm not sure it's been mentioned much yet that Cleo evidently released IOCs related to CVE-2024-50623 in October 2024, implying the older bug's been exploited for a minute. Would sure be helpful to know more about who was doing that exploiting, particularly now that Cl0p has claimed credit for last week's attack.

marreg@digitalcourage.social at 2024-12-20T17:42:57.000Z ##

CVE-2024-56337: Apache Tomcat: RCE due to TOCTOU issue in JSP compilation - CVE-2024-50379 mitigation was incomplete !

Severity: important

Affected versions:

- Apache Tomcat 11.0.0-M1 through 11.0.1
- Apache Tomcat 10.1.0-M1 through 10.1.33
- Apache Tomcat 9.0.0.M1 through 9.0.97

Description:

Time-of-check Time-of-use (TOCTOU) Race Condition vulnerability in Apache Tomcat.

This issue affects Apache Tomcat: from 11.0.0-M1 through 11.0.1, from 10.1.0-M1 through 10.1.33, from 9.0.0.M1 through 9.0.97.

The mitigation for CVE-2024-50379 was incomplete.

Tomcat 11.0.3, 10.1.35 and 9.0.99 onwards will include checks that sun.io.useCanonCaches is set appropriately before allowing the default servlet to be write enabled on a case insensitive file system. Tomcat will also set sun.io.useCanonCaches to false by default where it can.

References:

https://www.cve.org/CVERecord?id=CVE-2024-50379

##

CVE-2024-53677(CVSS UNKNOWN)

EPSS: 0.04%

updated 2024-12-20T18:35:12

30 posts

File upload logic is flawed vulnerability in Apache Struts. An attacker can manipulate file upload params to enable paths traversal and under some circumstances this can lead to uploading a malicious file which can be used to perform Remote Code Execution. This issue affects Apache Struts: from 2.0.0 before 6.4.0. Users are recommended to upgrade to version 6.4.0 at least and migrate to the new

todb at 2024-12-23T13:52:07.093Z ##

Near as I can tell, the activity around the #Struts2 bug,
CVE-2024-53677, is just ham-handed runs of some generalized PoC, and nobody's actually exploiting this yet (since exploitation would be very application/path specific).

Tell me I'm wrong!

(The PoC identified by SANS at https://isc.sans.edu/diary/31520 isn't specific to some particular application -- it's on the user to define upload_endpoint and assumes no auth or session or anything.)

##
catc0n at 2024-12-18T20:43:59.095Z ##

Almost exactly a year ago, Rapid7 put out a technical analysis of Apache #Struts 2 CVE-2023-50164 that said:

* Exploit payloads were going to need to be customized to the target

* It wasn't clear that there was any critical mass of remotely exploitable applications out of the box

* The reports of exploitation in the wild all appeared to be unsuccessful attempts rather than IRL compromises of production systems.

https://attackerkb.com/topics/pe3CCtOE81/cve-2023-50164/rapid7-analysis

Fast-forward to CVE-2024-53677 and we can repeat the above verbatim, with one pretty notable exception — the "fixed" version that ostensibly remediates the vulnerability actually doesn't, and code-level changes are required (to migrate away from the vulnerable file upload interceptor) to actually remediate it. Also the "fixed" release (6.4.0) appears to have gone out a year ago? No idea. Big ups to @fuzz for the analysis!

https://attackerkb.com/assessments/28f08c0a-702c-4ab0-99cb-eea00202fa2c

##
GossiTheDog@cyberplace.social at 2024-12-18T17:25:57.000Z ##

On CVE-2024-53677 (Struts vuln), it's following a very similar path to the Struts 2 vuln this time last year:

- Media are reporting it is being exploited in the wild. It isn't. People are spraying and praying - the exploit payloads don't work.

- People are posting a PoC for it. The PoC doesn't work. You'd have to make a vulnerable webapp, and then tailor the PoC to it.

Not to downplay it, just keep calm and patch. You may have noticed the internet didn't melt last time.

CCCS (Canada): Alert - CVE-2024-53677 - Vulnerability impacting Apache Struts 2
I see multiple government organizations emphasize the criticality of CVE-2024-53677 (CVSSv4: 9.5 critical) affecting both end-of-life and current versions of Apache Struts 2. A malicious actor can exploit this vulnerability to traverse system paths, upload malicious files, and perform remote code execution.

The Canadian Centre for Cyber Security (CCCS) is aware that a proof of concept (POC) exploit is available for this CVE.

catc0n at 2024-12-16T13:02:28.414Z ##

Full Rapid7 analysis of #Cleo CVE-2024-55956 now available c/o @stephenfewer. It's neither a patch bypass of CVE-2024-50623 nor part of a chain after all — totally new bug, different exploitation strategies across the two issues (though the same endpoint gets used either way).

I'm not sure it's been mentioned much yet that Cleo evidently released IOCs related to CVE-2024-50623 in October 2024, implying the older bug's been exploited for a minute. Would sure be helpful to know more about who was doing that exploiting, particularly now that Cl0p has claimed credit for last week's attack.

CVE-2024-12729
(8.8 HIGH)

EPSS: 0.04%

updated 2024-12-20T00:32:18

6 posts

A post-auth SQLi vulnerability in the User Portal allows authenticated users to execute code remotely in Sophos Firewall older than version 21.0 MR1 (21.0.1).

screaminggoat at 2024-12-20T16:02:58.403Z ##

Sophos security advisory 19 December 2024: Resolved Multiple Vulnerabilities in Sophos Firewall (CVE-2024-12727, CVE-2024-12728, CVE-2024-12729)

  • CVE-2024-12727 (9.8 critical) pre-auth SQL injection vulnerability in the email protection feature of Sophos Firewall
  • CVE-2024-12728 (9.8 critical) weak credentials vulnerability potentially allows privileged system access via SSH to Sophos Firewall
  • CVE-2024-12729 (8.8 high) post-auth code injection vulnerability in the User Portal allows authenticated users to execute code remotely in Sophos Firewall

Sophos has not observed these vulnerabilities to be exploited at this time.

#sophos #firewall #vulnerability #cve #infosec #cybersecurity

##
AAKL at 2024-12-20T14:46:34.694Z ##

If you missed this, Sophos has patched three vulnerabilities.

Resolved Multiple Vulnerabilities in Sophos Firewall (CVE-2024-12727, CVE-2024-12728, CVE-2024-12729) https://www.sophos.com/en-us/security-advisories/sophos-sa-20241219-sfos-rce @SophosXOps

More: https://thehackernews.com/2024/12/sophos-fixes-3-critical-firewall-flaws.html @thehackernews #cybersecurity #infosec

##
decio at 2024-12-20T09:31:45.161Z ##

Firewall #Sophos : 3 #vulnerabilites critiques corrigées (CVE-2024-12727, CVE-2024-12728, CVE-2024-12729)

CVE-2024-12727 (Critique)
Une vulnérabilité d'injection SQL pré-authentification dans la fonctionnalité de protection email.

Impact : Risque d'exécution de code à distance (RCE) si certaines configurations spécifiques (SPX activé + mode HA) sont en place.
Découverte : Signalée par un chercheur externe via le programme de bug bounty Sophos.

CVE-2024-12728 (Critique)
Un mot de passe SSH suggéré et non-aléatoire pour l'initialisation de clusters HA peut rester actif après déploiement.

Impact : Exposition d'un compte système privilégié si SSH est activé.
Découverte : Détection interne par Sophos.

CVE-2024-12729 (Haut)
Injection de code post-authentification via le Portail Utilisateur.

Impact : Utilisateurs authentifiés peuvent exécuter du code à distance.
Découverte : Signalée par un chercheur externe via le programme de bug bounty Sophos.

📌 Correctifs et recommandations :

Hotfixes disponibles : Appliqués automatiquement si l'option d'installation automatique est activée (paramètre par défaut).

Versions affectées : Sophos Firewall v21.0 GA et versions antérieures.

Remédiation : Vérifiez que vous utilisez une version corrigée ou mettez à jour vers la dernière version compatible (v21 MR1 ou plus récent).

🔒 Mesures de protection:

Désactiver l'accès WAN au Portail Utilisateur et à Webadmin : Utilisez des VPN ou Sophos Central pour la gestion à distance.

Restreindre l'accès SSH :
Limiter aux ports HA dédiés, physiquement séparés.
Reconfigurer HA avec une passphrase aléatoire et suffisamment longue.

"Sophos has not observed these vulnerabilities to be exploited at this time."
👇
https://www.sophos.com/en-us/security-advisories/sophos-sa-20241219-sfos-rce

#CyberVeille #CVE_2024_12727 #CVE_2024_12728 #CVE-2024-12729

Due to an unchecked buffer length, a specially crafted L2CAP packet can cause a buffer overflow. This buffer overflow triggers an assert, which results in a temporary denial of service.  If a watchdog timer is not enabled, a hard reset is required to recover the device.

1 repos

CVE-2024-12728
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 0.04%

updated 2024-12-19T21:31:22

8 posts

A weak credentials vulnerability potentially allows privileged system access via SSH to Sophos Firewall older than version 20.0 MR3 (20.0.3).

decio at 2024-12-20T09:31:45.161Z ##

Firewall #Sophos : 3 #vulnerabilites critiques corrigées (CVE-2024-12727, CVE-2024-12728, CVE-2024-12729)

CVE-2024-12727 (Critique)
Une vulnérabilité d'injection SQL pré-authentification dans la fonctionnalité de protection email.

Impact : Risque d'exécution de code à distance (RCE) si certaines configurations spécifiques (SPX activé + mode HA) sont en place.
Découverte : Signalée par un chercheur externe via le programme de bug bounty Sophos.

CVE-2024-12728 (Critique)
Un mot de passe SSH suggéré et non-aléatoire pour l'initialisation de clusters HA peut rester actif après déploiement.

Impact : Exposition d'un compte système privilégié si SSH est activé.
Découverte : Détection interne par Sophos.

CVE-2024-12729 (Haut)
Injection de code post-authentification via le Portail Utilisateur.

Impact : Utilisateurs authentifiés peuvent exécuter du code à distance.
Découverte : Signalée par un chercheur externe via le programme de bug bounty Sophos.

📌 Correctifs et recommandations :

Hotfixes disponibles : Appliqués automatiquement si l'option d'installation automatique est activée (paramètre par défaut).

Versions affectées : Sophos Firewall v21.0 GA et versions antérieures.

Remédiation : Vérifiez que vous utilisez une version corrigée ou mettez à jour vers la dernière version compatible (v21 MR1 ou plus récent).

🔒 Mesures de protection:

Désactiver l'accès WAN au Portail Utilisateur et à Webadmin : Utilisez des VPN ou Sophos Central pour la gestion à distance.

Restreindre l'accès SSH :
Limiter aux ports HA dédiés, physiquement séparés.
Reconfigurer HA avec une passphrase aléatoire et suffisamment longue.

"Sophos has not observed these vulnerabilities to be exploited at this time."
👇
https://www.sophos.com/en-us/security-advisories/sophos-sa-20241219-sfos-rce

screaminggoat at 2024-12-20T16:02:58.403Z ##

Sophos security advisory 19 December 2024: Resolved Multiple Vulnerabilities in Sophos Firewall (CVE-2024-12727, CVE-2024-12728, CVE-2024-12729)

  • CVE-2024-12727 (9.8 critical) pre-auth SQL injection vulnerability in the email protection feature of Sophos Firewall
  • CVE-2024-12728 (9.8 critical) weak credentials vulnerability potentially allows privileged system access via SSH to Sophos Firewall
  • CVE-2024-12729 (8.8 high) post-auth code injection vulnerability in the User Portal allows authenticated users to execute code remotely in Sophos Firewall

Sophos has not observed these vulnerabilities to be exploited at this time.

CVE-2024-50379
(9.8 CRITICAL)

EPSS: 0.04%

updated 2024-12-18T19:32:52

17 posts

Time-of-check Time-of-use (TOCTOU) Race Condition vulnerability during JSP compilation in Apache Tomcat permits an RCE on case insensitive file systems when the default servlet is enabled for write (non-default configuration). This issue affects Apache Tomcat: from 11.0.0-M1 through 11.0.1, from 10.1.0-M1 through 10.1.33, from 9.0.0.M1 through 9.0.97. Users are recommended to upgrade to version

https://github.com/v3153/CVE-2024-50379-POC

decio at 2024-12-20T09:02:15.028Z ##

Une #vulnerabilite critique, identifiée comme CVE-2024-50379, a été découverte dans Apache Tomcat. Cette faille est due à une condition de concurrence (race condition) lors de la compilation des JSP (JavaServer Pages) sur des systèmes de fichiers insensibles à la casse, tels que Windows.

Pour qu'un attaquant puisse exploiter cette vulnérabilité et exécuter du code à distance, deux conditions doivent être réunies :

  • Le servlet par défaut de Tomcat doit être configuré pour autoriser l'écriture, ce qui n'est pas la configuration par défaut

  • Le système doit utiliser un système de fichiers insensible à la casse, permettant à des fichiers comme "test.jsp" et "TEST.JSP" d'être traités de manière identique.

Il est recommandé de mettre à jour Apache Tomcat vers les versions corrigées (9.0.98, 10.1.34, 11.0.2) et de vérifier que le servlet par défaut n'autorise pas l'écriture, sauf si cela est absolument nécessaire.

[Advisory]
👇
https://lists.apache.org/thread/y6lj6q1xnp822g6ro70tn19sgtjmr80r

[PoC]
👇
https://github.com/iSee857/CVE-2024-50379-PoC/tree/main
👇
https://github.com/yiliufeng168/CVE-2024-50379-POC

Pour qu'un attaquant puisse exploiter cette vulnérabilité et exécuter du code à distance, deux conditions doivent être réunies :

  • Le servlet par défaut de Tomcat doit être configuré pour autoriser l'écriture, ce qui n'est pas la configuration par défaut

  • Le système doit utiliser un système de fichiers insensible à la casse, permettant à des fichiers comme "test.jsp" et "TEST.JSP" d'être traités de manière identique.

Il est recommandé de mettre à jour Apache Tomcat vers les versions corrigées (9.0.98, 10.1.34, 11.0.2) et de vérifier que le servlet par défaut n'autorise pas l'écriture, sauf si cela est absolument nécessaire.

#OSINT #ThreatIntel #CyberSecurity #cve_2024_50379

##
decio at 2024-12-20T09:02:15.028Z ##

Une #vulnerabilite critique, identifiée comme CVE-2024-50379, a été découverte dans Apache Tomcat. Cette faille est due à une condition de concurrence (race condition) lors de la compilation des JSP (JavaServer Pages) sur des systèmes de fichiers insensibles à la casse, tels que Windows.

Pour qu'un attaquant puisse exploiter cette vulnérabilité et exécuter du code à distance, deux conditions doivent être réunies :

  • Le servlet par défaut de Tomcat doit être configuré pour autoriser l'écriture, ce qui n'est pas la configuration par défaut

  • Le système doit utiliser un système de fichiers insensible à la casse, permettant à des fichiers comme "test.jsp" et "TEST.JSP" d'être traités de manière identique.

Il est recommandé de mettre à jour Apache Tomcat vers les versions corrigées (9.0.98, 10.1.34, 11.0.2) et de vérifier que le servlet par défaut n'autorise pas l'écriture, sauf si cela est absolument nécessaire.

##
marreg@digitalcourage.social at 2024-12-20T17:42:57.000Z ##

CVE-2024-56337: Apache Tomcat: RCE due to TOCTOU issue in JSP compilation - CVE-2024-50379 mitigation was incomplete !

Severity: important

Affected versions:

- Apache Tomcat 11.0.0-M1 through 11.0.1
- Apache Tomcat 10.1.0-M1 through 10.1.33
- Apache Tomcat 9.0.0.M1 through 9.0.97

Description:

Time-of-check Time-of-use (TOCTOU) Race Condition vulnerability in Apache Tomcat.

This issue affects Apache Tomcat: from 11.0.0-M1 through 11.0.1, from 10.1.0-M1 through 10.1.33, from 9.0.0.M1 through 9.0.97.

The mitigation for CVE-2024-50379 was incomplete.

Tomcat 11.0.3, 10.1.35 and 9.0.99 onwards will include checks that sun.io.useCanonCaches is set appropriately before allowing the default servlet to be write enabled on a case insensitive file system. Tomcat will also set sun.io.useCanonCaches to false by default where it can.

References:

https://www.cve.org/CVERecord?id=CVE-2024-50379
https://lists.apache.org/thread/b2b9qrgjrz1kvo4ym8y2wkfdvwoq6qbp
https://tomcat.apache.org/
https://www.cve.org/CVERecord?id=CVE-2024-56337

updated 2024-12-18T15:48:26

Versions of the package spatie/browsershot before 5.0.2 are vulnerable to Directory Traversal due to URI normalisation in the browser where the file:// check can be bypassed with file:\\. An attacker could read any file on the server by exploiting the normalization of \ into /.

Since it's already a ../ kind of day, how about another one in browsershot?

Edit to add the NVD link: https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2024-21547

This one is fun because the protocol checks only looked for file:// and could be bypassed by using file:\\.

##
screaminggoat at 2024-12-18T18:20:30.843Z ##

CVE-2023-34990 is credited to @hacks_zach of Horizon3.ai. This gave me a starting point for figuring out where to look for information. It's contained in Fortinet FortiWLM Deep-Dive, IOCs, and the Almost Story of the “Forti Forty” posted on 14 March 2024.

It was described as an unpatched vulnerability: "Unauthenticated Limited Log File Read – Allows retrieval of arbitrary log files which contain administrator session ID tokens" Check out the Path to Remote Code Execution #2 section for vulnerability details:

This vulnerability allows remote, unauthenticated attackers to access and abuse builtin functionality meant to read specific log files on the system via a crafted request to the /ems/cgi-bin/ezrf_lighttpd.cgi endpoint. This issue results from the lack of input validation on request parameters allowing an attacker to traverse directories and read any log file on the system.

Based on the details of the blog, I can confidently say that the new CVE and the blog's description of the vulnerability are almost certainly one and the same. Timeline puts the reporting at 585 days ago.

harrysintonen@infosec.exchange at 2024-12-15T13:18:26.000Z ##

@jos1264 This report is wrong. The vulnerability is not critical. It's low level vulnerability: https://curl.se/docs/CVE-2024-11053.html

##
harrysintonen@infosec.exchange at 2024-12-15T12:49:40.000Z ##

@hughsie @securestep9 In this particular case it's completely made up by CISA. I am the reporter of this vulnerability and I agree with the #curl project that this is not a critical vulnerability.

The issue here is that the score made up by CISA will trickle down to various automated systems. This can lead to effects downstream where systems will become unusable as they have unpatched supposedly critical vulnerabilities. We've seen this happen before.

Edit: The source of the wrong score is CISA ADP: https://github.com/cisagov/vulnrichment/blob/develop/2024/11xxx/CVE-2024-11053.json

Google Project Zero: The Qualcomm DSP Driver - Unexpectedly Excavating an Exploit
This blog post is a companion piece to Amnesty International's report (see parent toot above): a technical analysis of kernel panic logs generated by an in-the-wild (ITW) exploit, which led to the discovery of 6 vulnerabilities in a Qualcomm driver (one noted by Google Threat Analysis Group (TAG) as exploited in the wild). This blog post covers the details of the original artifacts, each of the bugs discovered, and the hypothesized ITW exploit strategy gleaned from the logs. Vulnerabilities explicitly mentioned are CVE-2024-38402, CVE-2024-21455, CVE-2024-33060, CVE-2024-49848, and CVE-2024-43047 (KEV). The Project Zero post ends with a rebuke of Qualcomm for not patching vulnerabilities under the industry standard 90 day deadline, with 49848 still being unfixed 145 days after being reported. "Past research has shown that chipset drivers for Android are a promising target for attackers, and this ITW exploit represents a meaningful real-world example of the negative ramifications that the current third-party vendor driver security posture poses to end-users"

catc0n at 2024-12-18T20:43:59.095Z ##

Almost exactly a year ago, Rapid7 put out a technical analysis of Apache #Struts 2 CVE-2023-50164 that said:

* Exploit payloads were going to need to be customized to the target

* It wasn't clear that there was any critical mass of remotely exploitable applications out of the box

* The reports of exploitation in the wild all appeared to be unsuccessful attempts rather than IRL compromises of production systems.

https://attackerkb.com/topics/pe3CCtOE81/cve-2023-50164/rapid7-analysis

Fast-forward to CVE-2024-53677 and we can repeat the above verbatim, with one pretty notable exception — the "fixed" version that ostensibly remediates the vulnerability actually doesn't, and code-level changes are required (to migrate away from the vulnerable file upload interceptor) to actually remediate it. Also the "fixed" release (6.4.0) appears to have gone out a year ago? No idea. Big ups to @fuzz for the analysis!

https://attackerkb.com/assessments/28f08c0a-702c-4ab0-99cb-eea00202fa2c

screaminggoat at 2024-12-16T22:14:41.280Z ##

CCB (Belgium): WARNING: CRITICAL VULNERABILITY IN APACHE STRUTS, CVE-2024-53677 CAN LEAD TO RCE, PATCH IMMEDIATELY!

Update 2024-12-16: PoC exploits have been released and active exploit attempts have been observed that match the PoC exploit code. Also, CVE-2024-53677 appears to be related to a similar, but older, vulnerability CVE-2023-50164 which may not have been completely patched

I'm not sure if this is the real proof of concept for CVE-2024-53677, but here's the link from the Bad Place™️: https://github.com/TAM-K592/CVE-2024-53677-S2-067

* The reports of exploitation in the wild all appeared to be unsuccessful attempts rather than IRL compromises of production systems.

https://attackerkb.com/topics/pe3CCtOE81/cve-2023-50164/rapid7-analysis

Fast-forward to CVE-2024-53677 and we can repeat the above verbatim, with one pretty notable exception — the "fixed" version that ostensibly remediates the vulnerability actually doesn't, and code-level changes are required (to migrate away from the vulnerable file upload interceptor) to actually remediate it. Also the "fixed" release (6.4.0) appears to have gone out a year ago? No idea. Big ups to @fuzz for the analysis!

https://attackerkb.com/assessments/28f08c0a-702c-4ab0-99cb-eea00202fa2c

##
screaminggoat@infosec.exchange at 2024-12-16T22:14:41.000Z ##

CCB (Belgium): WARNING: CRITICAL VULNERABILITY IN APACHE STRUTS, CVE-2024-53677 CAN LEAD TO RCE, PATCH IMMEDIATELY!
The Centre for Cybersecurity Belgium (CCB) goes one step further and says that it's actively exploited. 😑

Update 2024-12-16: PoC exploits have been released and active exploit attempts have been observed that match the PoC exploit code. Also, CVE-2024-53677 appears to be related to a similar, but older, vulnerability CVE-2023-50164 which may not have been completely patched

I'm not sure if this is the real proof of concept for CVE-2024-53677, but here's the link from the Bad Place™️: https://github.com/TAM-K592/CVE-2024-53677-S2-067

CVE-2016-9594
(8.1 HIGH)

EPSS: 0.85%

updated 2023-02-01T05:08:57

2 posts

curl before version 7.52.1 is vulnerable to an uninitialized random in libcurl's internal function that returns a good 32bit random value. Having a weak or virtually non-existent random value makes the operations that use it vulnerable.

bagder@mastodon.social at 2024-12-23T10:34:11.000Z ##

Eight years ago on this date, I had to publicly share this #curl security advisory as perhaps one of my lamest mistakes ever: https://curl.se/docs/CVE-2016-9594.html

We learn from our mistakes. Hopefully.

CVE-2021-20023
(4.9 MEDIUM)

EPSS: 93.33%

updated 2023-01-27T05:03:14

6 posts

SonicWall Email Security version 10.0.9.x contains a vulnerability that allows a post-authenticated attacker to read an arbitrary file on the remote host.

cR0w at 2024-12-19T18:47:19.847Z ##

@screaminggoat Heh. It's an old one and listed as already used by ransomware so I figured people should already have that one noted.

But I show it as 4.9 per NIST with a vector of CVSS:3.1/AV:N/AC:L/PR:H/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:N/A:N

https://nvd.nist.gov/vuln/detail/CVE-2021-20023

##
screaminggoat at 2024-12-19T18:41:35.578Z ##

@cR0w you gonna drop a CVE and make me work for the context? :blobtongue:

SonicWall's security advisory actually scores CVE-2021-20023 higher at 6.7 medium using the v3.0 vector: CVSS:3.0/AV:N/AC:L/PR:H/UI:N/S:U/C:H/I:L/A:H. Here is SonicWall's actual zero-day product notification, which links to FireEye (now Mandiant, part of Google Cloud): Zero-Day Exploits in SonicWall Email Security Lead to Enterprise Compromise

Combinations of all three exploits were leveraged interchangeably by the adversary to perform the following actions:

  1. Creation of a new Administrator account on the SonicWall ES device
  2. Exposure of the hashed passwords for existing, locally configured Administrative accounts
  3. The creation of a web shell in an arbitrary directory
  4. Real-time debugging of exploitation success and failure

Now THIS is the context of CVE-2021-20023. It really is about how an attacker leverages the vulnerability and not the CVSS score.

##
cR0w at 2024-12-19T18:29:37.916Z ##

Here's another fun ../ stat: There are currently 25 directory traversal CVEs in the CISA KEV catalog. One of them ( CVE-2021-20023 ) has a CVSS score of 4.9 . Point being that CVSS scores are a nice metric and all, especially for BINGO cards and such, but please read the actual write-ups. That will give you so much more context than the silly, often inaccurate numbers.

##
screaminggoat at 2024-12-16T16:32:27.160Z ##

Google Project Zero: The Qualcomm DSP Driver - Unexpectedly Excavating an Exploit
This blog post is a companion piece to Amnesty International's report (see parent toot above): a technical analysis of kernel panic logs generated by an in-the-wild (ITW) exploit, which led to the discovery of 6 vulnerabilities in a Qualcomm driver (one noted by Google Threat Analysis Group (TAG) as exploited in the wild). This blog post covers the details of the original artifacts, each of the bugs discovered, and the hypothesized ITW exploit strategy gleaned from the logs. Vulnerabilities explicitly mentioned are CVE-2024-38402, CVE-2024-21455, CVE-2024-33060, CVE-2024-49848, and CVE-2024-43047 (KEV). The Project Zero post ends with a rebuke of Qualcomm for not patching vulnerabilities under the industry standard 90 day deadline, with 49848 still being unfixed 145 days after being reported. "Past research has shown that chipset drivers for Android are a promising target for attackers, and this ITW exploit represents a meaningful real-world example of the negative ramifications that the current third-party vendor driver security posture poses to end-users"

#serbia #spyware #cellebrite #humanrights #privacy #zeroday #vulnerability #bia #novispy #spyware #infosec #cyberthreatintelligence #cybersecurity #CTI #qualcomm
